# obp-python
The Open Bank Project API v6.0.0 provides standardized banking APIs.

This Python package is automatically generated by the [OpenAPI Generator](https://openapi-generator.tech) project
from the [OBP-API](https://github.com/OpenBankProject/OBP-API) OpenAPI spec.

For more information, please visit [https://www.openbankproject.com](https://www.openbankproject.com)

## Requirements

Python 3.9+

## Installation & Usage

### pip install

Install from [PyPI](https://pypi.org/project/obp-python/):

```sh
pip install obp-python
```

### Install from GitHub

```sh
pip install "obp-python @ git+https://github.com/OpenBankProject/OBP-SDKs.git#subdirectory=sdks/python"
```

Or with Poetry:

```sh
poetry add "git+https://github.com/OpenBankProject/OBP-SDKs.git#subdirectory=sdks/python"
```

### Install from source

```sh
git clone https://github.com/OpenBankProject/OBP-SDKs.git
cd OBP-SDKs/sdks/python
pip install .
```

### Tests

Execute `pytest` to run the tests.

## Getting Started

```python
import os
import obp_python
from obp_python.api.bank_api import BankApi
from obp_python.rest import ApiException

configuration = obp_python.Configuration(
    host = "https://apisandbox.openbankproject.com"
)

# --- Option 1: DirectLogin ---
# Obtain a token via the DirectLogin endpoint, then:
configuration.api_key['DirectLogin'] = 'token="%s"' % os.environ["OBP_DIRECT_LOGIN_TOKEN"]

# --- Option 2: OAuth2 ---
# configuration.access_token = os.environ["OBP_ACCESS_TOKEN"]

# --- Option 3: GatewayLogin ---
# configuration.api_key['GatewayLogin'] = 'token="%s"' % os.environ["OBP_GATEWAY_LOGIN_TOKEN"]

with obp_python.ApiClient(configuration) as api_client:
    bank_api = BankApi(api_client)
    try:
        response = bank_api.o_bpv6_0_0_get_banks()
        for bank in response.banks or []:
            print(f"{bank.full_name} (id: {bank.bank_id})")
    except ApiException as e:
        print(f"API error: {e}")
```

<a id="documentation-for-authorization"></a>
## Documentation For Authorization


Authentication schemes defined for the API:
<a id="DirectLogin"></a>
### DirectLogin

- **Type**: API key
- **API key parameter name**: DirectLogin
- **Location**: HTTP header

<a id="GatewayLogin"></a>
### GatewayLogin

- **Type**: API key
- **API key parameter name**: Authorization
- **Location**: HTTP header

<a id="OAuth2"></a>
### OAuth2

- **Type**: OAuth
- **Flow**: accessCode
- **Authorization URL**: http://127.0.0.1:8080/oauth/authorize
- **Scopes**: N/A
